
## 23

```cpp
#ifÂ !defined(Â PTHREAD_HÂ )
#defineÂ PTHREAD_H

/*
Â *Â SeeÂ theÂ READMEÂ fileÂ forÂ anÂ explanationÂ ofÂ theÂ pthreads-win32Â version
Â *Â numberingÂ schemeÂ andÂ howÂ theÂ DLLÂ isÂ namedÂ etc.
Â */
#defineÂ PTW32_VERSIONÂ 2,9,1,0
#defineÂ PTW32_VERSION_STRINGÂ "2,Â 9,Â 1,Â 0\0"

/*Â ThereÂ areÂ threeÂ implementationsÂ ofÂ cancelÂ cleanup.
Â *Â NoteÂ thatÂ pthread.hÂ isÂ includedÂ inÂ bothÂ application
Â *Â compilationÂ unitsÂ andÂ alsoÂ internallyÂ forÂ theÂ library.
Â *Â TheÂ codeÂ hereÂ andÂ withinÂ theÂ libraryÂ aimsÂ toÂ work
Â *Â forÂ allÂ reasonableÂ combinationsÂ ofÂ environments.
Â *
Â *Â TheÂ threeÂ implementationsÂ are:
Â *
Â *Â Â Â WIN32Â SEH
Â *Â Â Â C
Â *Â Â Â C++
Â *
Â *Â PleaseÂ noteÂ thatÂ exitingÂ aÂ push/popÂ blockÂ via
Â *Â "return",Â "exit",Â "break",&nbs***bsp;"continue"Â will
Â *Â leadÂ toÂ differentÂ behaviourÂ amongstÂ applications
Â *Â dependingÂ uponÂ whetherÂ theÂ libraryÂ wasÂ built
Â *Â usingÂ SEH,Â C++,&nbs***bsp;C.Â ForÂ example,Â aÂ libraryÂ built
Â *Â withÂ SEHÂ willÂ callÂ theÂ cleanupÂ routine,Â whileÂ both
Â *Â C++Â andÂ CÂ builtÂ versionsÂ willÂ not.
Â */

/*
Â *Â DefineÂ defaultsÂ forÂ cleanupÂ code.
Â *Â Note:Â UnlessÂ theÂ buildÂ explicitlyÂ definesÂ oneÂ ofÂ theÂ following,Â then
Â *Â weÂ defaultÂ toÂ standardÂ CÂ styleÂ cleanup.Â ThisÂ styleÂ usesÂ setjmp/longjmp
Â *Â inÂ theÂ cancelationÂ andÂ threadÂ exitÂ implementationsÂ andÂ thereforeÂ won't
Â *Â doÂ stackÂ unwindingÂ ifÂ linkedÂ toÂ applicationsÂ thatÂ haveÂ itÂ (e.g.
Â *Â C++Â apps).Â ThisÂ isÂ currentlyÂ consistentÂ withÂ most/allÂ commercialÂ Unix
Â *Â POSIXÂ threadsÂ implementations.
Â */
#ifÂ !defined(Â __CLEANUP_SEHÂ )Â &&Â !defined(Â __CLEANUP_CXXÂ )Â &&Â !defined(Â __CLEANUP_CÂ )
#Â defineÂ __CLEANUP_C
#endif

#ifÂ defined(Â __CLEANUP_SEHÂ )Â &&Â (Â !defined(Â _MSC_VERÂ )Â &&Â !defined(PTW32_RC_MSC))
#errorÂ ERRORÂ [__FILE__,Â lineÂ __LINE__]:Â SEHÂ isÂ notÂ supportedÂ forÂ thisÂ compiler.
#endif

/*
Â *Â StopÂ hereÂ ifÂ weÂ areÂ beingÂ includedÂ byÂ theÂ resourceÂ compiler.
Â */
#ifÂ !defined(RC_INVOKED)

#undefÂ PTW32_LEVEL

#ifÂ defined(_POSIX_SOURCE)
#defineÂ PTW32_LEVELÂ 0
/*Â EarlyÂ POSIXÂ */
#endif

#ifÂ defined(_POSIX_C_SOURCE)Â &&Â _POSIX_C_SOURCEÂ >=Â 199309
#undefÂ PTW32_LEVEL
#defineÂ PTW32_LEVELÂ 1
/*Â IncludeÂ 1b,Â 1cÂ andÂ 1dÂ */
#endif

#ifÂ defined(INCLUDE_NP)
#undefÂ PTW32_LEVEL
#defineÂ PTW32_LEVELÂ 2
/*Â IncludeÂ Non-PortableÂ extensionsÂ */
#endif

#defineÂ PTW32_LEVEL_MAXÂ 3

#ifÂ (Â defined(_POSIX_C_SOURCE)Â &&Â _POSIX_C_SOURCEÂ >=Â 200112Â )Â Â ||Â !defined(PTW32_LEVEL)
#defineÂ PTW32_LEVELÂ PTW32_LEVEL_MAX
/*Â IncludeÂ everythingÂ */
#endif

#ifÂ defined(_UWIN)
#Â Â Â defineÂ HAVE_STRUCT_TIMESPECÂ 1
#Â Â Â defineÂ HAVE_SIGNAL_HÂ Â Â Â Â Â Â Â 1
#Â Â Â undefÂ HAVE_PTW32_CONFIG_H
#Â Â Â pragmaÂ comment(lib,Â "pthread")
#endif

/*
Â *Â -------------------------------------------------------------
Â *
Â *
Â *Â Module:Â pthread.h
Â *
Â *Â Purpose:
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â ProvidesÂ anÂ implementationÂ ofÂ PThreadsÂ basedÂ uponÂ the
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â standard:
Â *
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â POSIXÂ 1003.1-2001
Â *Â Â and
Â *Â Â Â Â TheÂ SingleÂ UnixÂ SpecificationÂ versionÂ 3
Â *
Â *Â Â Â Â (theseÂ twoÂ areÂ equivalent)
Â *
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â inÂ orderÂ toÂ enhanceÂ codeÂ portabilityÂ betweenÂ Windows,
Â *Â Â variousÂ commercialÂ UnixÂ implementations,Â andÂ Linux.
Â *
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â SeeÂ theÂ ANNOUNCEÂ fileÂ forÂ aÂ fullÂ listÂ ofÂ conforming
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â routinesÂ andÂ definedÂ constants,Â andÂ aÂ listÂ ofÂ missing
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â routinesÂ andÂ constantsÂ notÂ definedÂ inÂ thisÂ implementation.
Â *
Â *Â Authors:
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â ThereÂ haveÂ beenÂ manyÂ contributorsÂ toÂ thisÂ library.
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â TheÂ initialÂ implementationÂ wasÂ contributedÂ by
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â JohnÂ Bossom,Â andÂ severalÂ othersÂ haveÂ providedÂ major
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â sections&nbs***bsp;revisionsÂ ofÂ partsÂ ofÂ theÂ implementation.
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â OftenÂ significantÂ effortÂ hasÂ beenÂ contributedÂ to
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â findÂ andÂ fixÂ importantÂ bugsÂ andÂ otherÂ problemsÂ to
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â improveÂ theÂ reliabilityÂ ofÂ theÂ library,Â whichÂ sometimes
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â isÂ notÂ reflectedÂ inÂ theÂ amountÂ ofÂ codeÂ whichÂ changedÂ as
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â result.
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â AsÂ muchÂ asÂ possible,Â theÂ contributorsÂ areÂ acknowledged
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â inÂ theÂ ChangeLogÂ fileÂ inÂ theÂ sourceÂ codeÂ distribution
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â whereÂ theirÂ changesÂ areÂ notedÂ inÂ detail.
Â *
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â ContributorsÂ areÂ listedÂ inÂ theÂ CONTRIBUTORSÂ file.
Â *
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â AsÂ usual,Â allÂ bouquetsÂ goÂ toÂ theÂ contributors,Â andÂ all
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â brickbatsÂ goÂ toÂ theÂ projectÂ maintainer.
Â *
Â *Â Maintainer:
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â TheÂ codeÂ baseÂ forÂ thisÂ projectÂ isÂ coordinatedÂ and
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â eventuallyÂ pre-tested,Â packaged,Â andÂ madeÂ availableÂ by
Â *
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â RossÂ JohnsonÂ <rpj@callisto.canberra.edu.au>
Â *
Â *Â QAÂ Testers:
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â Ultimately,Â theÂ libraryÂ isÂ testedÂ inÂ theÂ realÂ worldÂ by
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â aÂ hostÂ ofÂ competentÂ andÂ demandingÂ scientistsÂ and
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â engineersÂ whoÂ reportÂ bugsÂ and/orÂ provideÂ solutions
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â whichÂ areÂ thenÂ fixed&nbs***bsp;incorporatedÂ intoÂ subsequent
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â versionsÂ ofÂ theÂ library.Â EachÂ timeÂ aÂ bugÂ isÂ fixed,Â a
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â testÂ caseÂ isÂ writtenÂ toÂ proveÂ theÂ fixÂ andÂ ensure
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â thatÂ laterÂ changesÂ toÂ theÂ codeÂ don'tÂ reintroduceÂ the
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â sameÂ error.Â TheÂ numberÂ ofÂ testÂ casesÂ isÂ slowlyÂ growing
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â andÂ thereforeÂ soÂ isÂ theÂ codeÂ reliability.
Â *
Â *Â Compliance:
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â SeeÂ theÂ fileÂ ANNOUNCEÂ forÂ theÂ listÂ ofÂ implemented
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â andÂ not-implementedÂ routinesÂ andÂ definedÂ options.
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â OfÂ course,Â theseÂ areÂ allÂ definedÂ isÂ thisÂ fileÂ asÂ well.
Â *
Â *Â WebÂ site:
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â TheÂ sourceÂ codeÂ andÂ otherÂ informationÂ aboutÂ thisÂ library
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â areÂ availableÂ from
Â *
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â http://sources.redhat.com/pthreads-win32/
Â *
Â *Â -------------------------------------------------------------
Â */

/*Â TryÂ toÂ avoidÂ includingÂ windows.hÂ */
#ifÂ (defined(__MINGW64__)Â ||Â defined(__MINGW32__))Â &&Â defined(__cplusplus)

#endifÂ Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â /*Â __cplusplusÂ */

/*
Â *Â -------------------------------------------------------------
Â *
Â *Â POSIXÂ 1003.1-2001Â Options
Â *Â =========================
Â *
Â *Â OptionsÂ areÂ normallyÂ setÂ inÂ <unistd.h>,Â whichÂ isÂ notÂ provided
Â *Â withÂ pthreads-win32.
Â *
Â *Â ForÂ conformanceÂ withÂ theÂ SingleÂ UnixÂ SpecificationÂ (versionÂ 3),Â allÂ ofÂ the
Â *Â optionsÂ belowÂ areÂ defined,Â andÂ haveÂ aÂ valueÂ ofÂ eitherÂ -1Â (notÂ supported)
Â *&nbs***bsp;200112LÂ (supported).
Â *
Â *Â TheseÂ optionsÂ canÂ neitherÂ beÂ leftÂ undefinedÂ norÂ haveÂ aÂ valueÂ ofÂ 0,Â because
Â *Â eitherÂ indicatesÂ thatÂ sysconf(),Â whichÂ isÂ notÂ implemented,Â mayÂ beÂ usedÂ at
Â *Â runtimeÂ toÂ checkÂ theÂ statusÂ ofÂ theÂ option.
Â *
Â *Â _POSIX_THREADSÂ (==Â 200112L)
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â IfÂ ==Â 200112L,Â youÂ canÂ useÂ threads
Â *
Â *Â _POSIX_THREAD_ATTR_STACKSIZEÂ (==Â 200112L)
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â IfÂ ==Â 200112L,Â youÂ canÂ controlÂ theÂ sizeÂ ofÂ aÂ thread's
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â stack
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â pthread_attr_getstacksize
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â pthread_attr_setstacksize
Â *
Â *Â _POSIX_THREAD_ATTR_STACKADDRÂ (==Â -1)
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â IfÂ ==Â 200112L,Â youÂ canÂ allocateÂ andÂ controlÂ aÂ thread's
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â stack.Â IfÂ notÂ supported,Â theÂ followingÂ functions
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â willÂ returnÂ ENOSYS,Â indicatingÂ theyÂ areÂ not
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â supported:
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â pthread_attr_getstackaddr
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â pthread_attr_setstackaddr
Â *
Â *Â _POSIX_THREAD_PRIORITY_SCHEDULINGÂ (==Â -1)
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â IfÂ ==Â 200112L,Â youÂ canÂ useÂ realtimeÂ scheduling.
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â ThisÂ optionÂ indicatesÂ thatÂ theÂ behaviourÂ ofÂ some
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â implementedÂ functionsÂ conformsÂ toÂ theÂ additionalÂ TPS
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â requirementsÂ inÂ theÂ standard.Â E.g.Â rwlocksÂ favour
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â writersÂ overÂ readersÂ whenÂ threadsÂ haveÂ equalÂ priority.
Â *
Â *Â _POSIX_THREAD_PRIO_INHERITÂ (==Â -1)
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â IfÂ ==Â 200112L,Â youÂ canÂ createÂ priorityÂ inheritance
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â mutexes.
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â pthread_mutexattr_getprotocolÂ +
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â pthread_mutexattr_setprotocolÂ +
Â *
Â *Â _POSIX_THREAD_PRIO_PROTECTÂ (==Â -1)
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â IfÂ ==Â 200112L,Â youÂ canÂ createÂ priorityÂ ceilingÂ mutexes
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â IndicatesÂ theÂ availabilityÂ of:
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â pthread_mutex_getprioceiling
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â pthread_mutex_setprioceiling
Â *Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â pthread_mutexattr_getprioceiling

#ifÂ defined(__cplusplus)

/*
Â *Â InternalÂ exceptions

/*Â FIXME:Â ThisÂ isÂ onlyÂ requiredÂ ifÂ theÂ libraryÂ wasÂ builtÂ usingÂ SEHÂ */
/*
Â *Â GetÂ internalÂ SEHÂ tag
Â */
PTW32_DLLPORTÂ DWORDÂ PTW32_CDECLÂ ptw32_get_exception_services_code(void);

#endifÂ /*Â PTW32_LEVELÂ >=Â PTW32_LEVEL_MAXÂ */

#ifÂ !defined(PTW32_BUILD)

#ifÂ defined(__CLEANUP_SEH)

/*
Â *Â RedefineÂ theÂ SEHÂ __exceptÂ keywordÂ toÂ ensureÂ thatÂ applications
Â *Â propagateÂ ourÂ internalÂ exceptionsÂ upÂ toÂ theÂ library'sÂ internalÂ handlers.
Â */
#defineÂ __except(Â EÂ )Â \
Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â __except(Â (Â GetExceptionCode()Â ==Â ptw32_get_exception_services_code()Â )Â \
Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â ?Â EXCEPTION_CONTINUE_SEARCHÂ :Â (Â EÂ )Â )

#endifÂ /*Â __CLEANUP_SEHÂ */

#ifÂ defined(__CLEANUP_CXX)

/*
Â *Â RedefineÂ theÂ C++Â catchÂ keywordÂ toÂ ensureÂ thatÂ applications
Â *Â propagateÂ ourÂ internalÂ exceptionsÂ upÂ toÂ theÂ library'sÂ internalÂ handlers.
Â */
#ifÂ defined(_MSC_VER)
Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â /*
Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â *Â WARNING:Â ReplaceÂ anyÂ 'catch(Â ...Â )'Â withÂ 'PtW32CatchAll'
Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â *Â ifÂ youÂ wantÂ Pthread-Win32Â cancelationÂ andÂ pthread_exitÂ toÂ work.
Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â */

#ifÂ !defined(PtW32NoCatchWarn)

#pragmaÂ message("SpecifyÂ \"/DPtW32NoCatchWarn\"Â compilerÂ flagÂ toÂ skipÂ thisÂ message.")
#pragmaÂ message("------------------------------------------------------------------")
#pragmaÂ message("WhenÂ compilingÂ applicationsÂ withÂ MSVC++Â andÂ C++Â exceptionÂ handling:")
#pragmaÂ message("Â Â ReplaceÂ anyÂ 'catch(Â ...Â )'Â inÂ routinesÂ calledÂ fromÂ POSIXÂ threads")
#pragmaÂ message("Â Â withÂ 'PtW32CatchAll'&nbs***bsp;'CATCHALL'Â ifÂ youÂ wantÂ POSIXÂ thread")
#pragmaÂ message("Â Â cancelationÂ andÂ pthread_exitÂ toÂ work.Â ForÂ example:")
#pragmaÂ message("")
#pragmaÂ message("Â Â Â Â #ifÂ defined(PtW32CatchAll)")
#pragmaÂ message("Â Â Â Â Â Â PtW32CatchAll")
#pragmaÂ message("Â Â Â Â #else")
#pragmaÂ message("Â Â Â Â Â Â catch(...)")
#pragmaÂ message("Â Â Â Â #endif")
#pragmaÂ message("Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â {")
#pragmaÂ message("Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â /*Â CatchallÂ blockÂ processingÂ */")
#pragmaÂ message("Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â }")
#pragmaÂ message("------------------------------------------------------------------")

#endif

#defineÂ PtW32CatchAllÂ \
Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â catch(Â ptw32_exceptionÂ &Â )Â {Â throw;Â }Â \
Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â catch(Â ...Â )

#elseÂ /*Â _MSC_VERÂ */

#defineÂ catch(Â EÂ )Â \
Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â catch(Â ptw32_exceptionÂ &Â )Â {Â throw;Â }Â \
Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â catch(Â EÂ )

#endifÂ /*Â _MSC_VERÂ */

#endifÂ /*Â __CLEANUP_CXXÂ */

#endifÂ /*Â !Â PTW32_BUILDÂ */

#ifÂ defined(__cplusplus)
}Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â /*Â EndÂ ofÂ externÂ "C"Â */
#endifÂ Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â /*Â __cplusplusÂ */

#ifÂ defined(PTW32__HANDLE_DEF)
#Â undefÂ HANDLE
#endif
#ifÂ defined(PTW32__DWORD_DEF)
#Â undefÂ DWORD
```
